)@@G@@OGIC                       *******  @H@@@!. *******      - ADD INPUT STRHD
)@@G@@ING VARIATIONS                         *******  @H@@@\. *******      - PHE
)@@G@@ROCESS ANY SDF FILE (EVEN IF NOT PRINT FILE)       *******  @H@@@!. ****HF
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  HG
)@@G@@@H@@@!. ****************************************************************HH
)@@G@@**********  @E@@@!$(1),ST   LIPROC$                     . INVOKE 'LI' PRHI
)@@G@@OCS   @E@@@!          TEP       A5,(1*/('Z'-'L')) . INIT 'L' OPTION KEY HJ
)@@G@@@ @@@!          S         A5,LOPT   @E@@@!          TEP       A5,(1*/('ZHK
)@@G@@'-'R')) . INIT 'R' OPTION KEY @ @@@!          S         A5,ROPT   @G@@@!HL
)@@G@@          AN,U      A4,6              . CALCULATE BATCH KEY = RUN TYPE-6HM
)@@G@@@F@@@!          S         A4,BATCH          . BATCH=0 FOR BATCH RUN     HN
)@@G@@@F@@@!          LMJ       X11,PREPF$        . PROCESS INPUT PARAMETERS  HO
)@@G@@@C@@@!          ERR$                        . ERROR   @G@@@!          TEHP
)@@G@@ST                        . INVOKE TEST FACILITY IF @MASM,T @E@@@!      HQ
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,IDLINE$       . GENERATE SIGN-ON    @C@@@!          PRHR
)@@G@@INT$    IDBUFF,8          . PRINT IT@D@@@!          PRINT$    0,0,1     HS
)@@G@@        . SKIP A LINE   @G@@@!          L,U       X1,IMAGE          . INHT
)@@G@@ITILIAZE PTRS FOR STRING INPUT@ @@@!          L,U       X2,HDBUFF @ @@@!HU
)@@G@@          L         X3,(1,0)  @E@@@!LOOP1     READ$     IMAGE,INIT      HV
)@@G@@  . READ NEXT STRING    @D@@@!          L,U       A3,0,A0           . WOHW
)@@G@@RD COUNT    @ @@@!          LXI       A0,A3     @ @@@!          LXM,U   HX
)@@G@@  A0,IMAGE  @A@@@!          A         A0,(0100,0)     @ @@@!          TNHY
)@@G@@Z       BATCH     @F@@@!          PRINT$                      . ECHO INPHZ
)@@G@@UT STRING IF BATCH@G@@@!          MSI,U     A3,6              . CONVERT IA
)@@G@@WORD COUNT TO BYTE COUNT@G@@@!LOOP2     AN,U      A3,1              . CAIB
)@@G@@LCULATE ACTUAL BYTE COUNT     @G@@@!          LXI       X1,A3           IC
)@@G@@  .   BY SUBTRACTING TRAILING BLANKS@ @@@!          LMJ       X11,BGET  ID
)@@G@@@ @@@!          TNE,U     A0,' '    @ @@@!          J         LOOP2     IE
)@@G@@@G@@@!          L,U       A0,1,A3           . MOVE INPUT STRING TO HDBUFIF
)@@G@@F     @^@@@!          LXI,U     X1,0@ @@@!          LMJ       X11,BMOVE IG
)@@G@@@G@@@!          S,S2      A0,HEAD,X3        . STORE BYTE COUNT IN HEAD TIH
)@@G@@ABLE  @E@@@!          L         A1,X2             . GET STARTING BYTE # II
)@@G@@@ @@@!          SSL       A1,18     @E@@@!          S,S1      A1,HEAD,*XIJ
)@@G@@3       . STORE IN HEAD TABLE @F@@@!          A         A1,A0           IK
)@@G@@  . UPDATE HDBUFF POINTER     @ @@@!          LXI       X2,A1     @F@@@!IL
)@@G@@          INC       NHEAD             . INCREMENT HEAD TABLE COUNT@#@@@!IM
)@@G@@          NOP     @E@@@!          S         X2,X4             . SAVE HDBIN
)@@G@@UFF PTR     @H@@@!          L,U       X2,ARROW          . SEARCH FOR AN IO
)@@G@@ARROW IN INPUT (->)     @ @@@!          L,U       A1,1,A3   @^@@@!      IP
)@@G@@    L,U       A2,2@A@@@!          LMJ       X11,FINDFIELD   @F@,@!      IQ
)@@G@@    J         CONT0A            . NONE FOUND, NORMAL CASE   @F@@@,      IR
)@@G@@    J         CONT2             . NONE FOUND, NORMAL CASE   @G@@@!      IS
)@@G@@    TZ        A0                . IS ARROW IN BEGINNING OF STRING?@B@,@!IT
)@@G@@          J         CONT0             . NO@B@@@,          J         CONTIU
)@@G@@1             . NO@D@@@!          L,T1      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . YES, GETIV
)@@G@@ SC,NC@I@@@!          A,U       A0,0176           . INCREMENT SC BY 2 ANIW
)@@G@@D DECREMENT NC BY 2     @F@@@!          S,T2      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . MOIX
)@@G@@VE TO 2ND STRING DESCR  @F@@@!          SZ,T1     HEAD-1,X3         . ZEIY
)@@G@@RO 1ST STRING DESCR     @ @,@!          J         CONT0A    @ @@@,      IZ
)@@G@@    J         CONT2     @G@,@!CONT0     S,S2      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . CHJA
)@@G@@ANGE BYTE COUNT FOR 1ST STRING@G@@@,CONT1     S,S2      A0,HEAD-1,X3    JB
)@@G@@  . CHANGE BYTE COUNT FOR 1ST STRING@F@@@!          TE,U      A3,1,A0   JC
)@@G@@        . IS ARROW AT END OF STRING?@B@@@!          J         $+3       JD
)@@G@@        . NO@F@@@!          SNZ,T2    HEAD-1,X3         . SET 2ND STRINGJE
)@@G@@ DESCR TO -0@ @,@!          J         CONT0A    @ @@@,          J       JF
)@@G@@  CONT2     @F@@@!          A,S1      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . GENERATE STRINJG
)@@G@@G 2 DESCR   @^@@@!          A,U       A0,2@A@@@!          S,S3      A0,HJH
)@@G@@EAD-1,X3    @A@@@!          AN,S2     A3,HEAD-1,X3    @^@@@!          ANJI
)@@G@@,U      A3,1@A@@@!          S,S4      A3,HEAD-1,X3    @E@,@!CONT0A    L JJ
)@@G@@        X2,X4             . RESTORE HDBUFF PTR  @E@@@,CONT2     L       JK
)@@G@@  X2,X4             . RESTORE HDBUFF PTR  @F@@@!          J         LOOPJL
)@@G@@1             . PROCESS NEXT INPUT STRING @H@@@!INIT      L,U       A0,FJM
)@@G@@CT            . INITIALIZE PRINT FILE FOR READING     @ @@@!          LXJN
)@@G@@I,U     X11,PIRCB$@A@@@!          LIJ       X11,BSDFIO$     @D@@@!      JO
)@@G@@    J         ERR2              . READ ERROR    @D@@@!          SZ      JP
)@@G@@  SWAP              . CLEAR SWAP KEY@E@@@!LOOP3     L,U       A0,FCT    JQ
)@@G@@        . READ NEXT SDF IMAGE @ @@@!          LXI,U     X11,PIRCB$@ @@@!JR
)@@G@@          LIJ       X11,BSDFI$@D@@@!          J         ERR2            JS
)@@G@@  . READ ERROR    @D@@@!          J         END               . END OF SJT
)@@G@@DF    @E@@@!          L         A1,CONTROL        . GET CONTROL WORD    JU
)@@G@@@F@@@!          JP        A1,DATA           . CHECK IF DATA CONTROL     JV
)@@G@@@H@@@!          L,S1      A0,CONTROL        . NO, WHAT KIND OF SDF CONTRJW
)@@G@@OL IS IT?   @E@@@!          TE,U      A0,050            . IS IT SDF HEADJX
)@@G@@ER?   @B@,@!          J         CONT1             . NO@B@@@,          J JY
)@@G@@        CONT3             . NO@B@1@\          L         A0,(PF 1,NMESS4,JZ
)@@G@@MESS4)@G@\@!          L,H1      A0,CONTROL        . IS IMAGE THE SDF PRIKA
)@@G@@NT HEADER?  @G@@@\          L,H1      A1,CONTROL        . IS IMAGE THE SKB
)@@G@@DF PRINT HEADER?  @A@\@!          TE        A0,(0501125)    @A@1@\      KC
)@@G@@    TE        A1,(0501125)    @A@@@1          TNE       A1,(0501125)    KD
)@@G@@@^@@@1          J         $+4 @F@\@!          J         ERR1            KE
)@@G@@  . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEADER  @F@1@\          PRINT$                    KF
)@@G@@  . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEADER  @F@@@1          PRINT$    MESS4,NMESS4    KG
)@@G@@  . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEADER  @ @@@1          J         LOOP3     @F@@@!KH
)@@G@@          TNZ       LOPT              . IF 'L' OPTION, PRINT LABEL@ @@@!KI
)@@G@@          J         LOOP3     @H@@@!          PRINT$    LABEL,NLABEL,2  KJ
)@@G@@  . 'PRINT FILE HAS FOLLOWING LABEL ...'  @F@@@!          E$DIT     EPKTKK
)@@G@@              . PRINT LABEL INFORMATION   @ @@@!          E$MSG     RUNIKL
)@@G@@D     @ @@@!          E$FD1     IMAGE+3   @^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   KM
)@@G@@@ @@@!          E$MSG     USERID    @ @@@!          E$FD2     IMAGE+5   KN
)@@G@@@^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$MSG     PARTNO    @A@@@!KO
)@@G@@          E$DECV    CONTROL,,S4     @^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!KP
)@@G@@          E$MSG     INDEV     @ @@@!          E$FD1     IMAGE+2   @^@@@!KQ
)@@G@@          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$MSG     FILEN     @ @@@!      KR
)@@G@@    E$FD2     IMAGE     @^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$KS
)@@G@@MSG     CREATE    @ @@@!          E$TIME    IMAGE+4   @^@@@!          E$KT
)@@G@@SKIP    1   @ @@@!          E$DAY3    IMAGE+4   @D@@@!          E$PRINT KU
)@@G@@  2                 . PRINT LABEL   @D@@@!          PRINT$    0,0,1     KV
)@@G@@        . SKIP A LINE   @ @@@!          J         LOOP3     @D@,@!CONT1 KW
)@@G@@    TE,U      A0,060            . PRINT CONTROL?@D@@@,CONT3     TE,U    KX
)@@G@@  A0,060            . PRINT CONTROL?@ @@@!          J         LOOP3     KY
)@@G@@@H@@@!          L,S2      A0,CONTROL        . GET # OF WDS IN PRINT CONTKZ
)@@G@@ROL IMAGE   @H@@@!          JZ        A0,LOOP3          . IF NO DATA, FILA
)@@G@@ND NEXT CONTROL IMAGE   @D@@@!          S         A0,NWDS           . SALB
)@@G@@VE # OF WDS @E@@@!          MSI,U     A0,6              . CONVERT TO CHALC
)@@G@@RS    @C@@@!          S         A0,NCHAR          . SAVE    @D@@@!      LD
)@@G@@    L,S6      X3,CONTROL        . GET CODE TYPE @E@@@!          S,H1    LE
)@@G@@  X3,BASCII         . STORE FOR BYTESUB   @ @@@!          SZ        PRINLF
)@@G@@T     @ @@@!          L,U       X1,IMAGE  @ @@@!          L,U       X2,PLG
)@@G@@RINT  @ @@@!          L         R1,A0     @ @@@!          L,U       R2,1LH
)@@G@@2     @E@@@!          LMJ       X11,GETSFIELD     . GET NEXT SUBFIELD   LI
)@@G@@@E@@@!          J         LOOP3             . ALL BLANK, SKIP     @A@@@!LJ
)@@G@@          L         A0,('H@@@@@')   @F@@@!          TNE       A0,PRINT  LK
)@@G@@        . HEADING PRINT CONTROL?    @C@,@!          J         CONT2     LL
)@@G@@        . YES     @C@@@,          J         CONT4             . YES     LM
)@@G@@@F@@@!          TNZ       KPRINT            . NO, IS PRINT KEY SET?     LN
)@@G@@@C@@@!          J         LOOP3             . NO, SKIP@F@,@!          J LO
)@@G@@        CONT5             . YES, SUBMIT PRINT CONTROL @F@@@,          J LP
)@@G@@        CONT9             . YES, SUBMIT PRINT CONTROL @F@,@!CONT2     L LQ
)@@G@@        A0,(PF -0,0,0)    . WAS A REPORT JUST PRINTED?@F@@@,CONT4     L LR
)@@G@@        A0,(PF -0,0,0)    . WAS A REPORT JUST PRINTED?@ @@@!          TZLS
)@@G@@        KPRINT    @E@@@!          PRINT$                      . YES, STALT
)@@G@@RT NEW PAGE @E@@@!          SZ        KPRINT            . CLEAR PRINT KELU
)@@G@@Y     @D@@@!          SZ        KHEAD             . CLEAR HEAD KEY@G@@@!LV
)@@G@@          TNZ       LOPT              . IF 'L' OPTION, PRINT HEADING    LW
)@@G@@@ @,@!          J         CONT3     @ @@@,          J         CONT5     LX
)@@G@@@^@@@!          SZ        A0  @ @@@!          LXI       A0,NWDS   @A@@@!LY
)@@G@@          A         A0,(0100,IMAGE) @ @@@!          EX        EPRINT,X3 LZ
)@@G@@@F@,@!CONT3     TZ        PRINTALL          . IS PRINT ALL KEY SET?     MA
)@@G@@@F@@@,CONT5     TZ        PRINTALL          . IS PRINT ALL KEY SET?     MB
)@@G@@@F@@@!          J         MATCH             . YES, ALL HEADINGS MATCH   MC
)@@G@@@H@@@!          L         X5,(1,0)          . COMPARE EACH INPUT HEADINGMD
)@@G@@ TO IMAGE   @ @@@!          L,U       X2,HDBUFF @E@@@!LOOP4     TNZ     ME
)@@G@@  HEAD,X5           . SKIP ZEROED HEADINGS@ @@@!          J         ELOOMF
)@@G@@P4    @D@@@,          SP1       KHEAD             . SET HEAD KEY  @G@@@!MG
)@@G@@          TZ,S4     HEAD,X5           . NORMAL CASE (SINGLE HEADING)?   MH
)@@G@@@B@,@!          J         CONT3A            . NO@B@@@,          J       MI
)@@G@@  CONT6             . NO@E@@@!          L,T1      A1,HEAD,X5        . YEMJ
)@@G@@S, LOOK FOR MATCH @ @@@!          LMJ       X10,SLIDE @F@@@!          J MK
)@@G@@        ELOOP4            . NO MATCH, TRY NEXT HEADING@^@@@,          TNML
)@@G@@Z       ROPT@D@,@!          SP1       KPRINT            . SET PRINT KEY MM
)@@G@@@D@,@!          SZ        HEAD,X5           . CLEAR ENTRY   @G@@@,      MN
)@@G@@    SZ        HEAD,X5           . CLEAR ENTRY IF NOT 'R' OPTION   @ @@@!MO
)@@G@@          J         MATCH     @D@,@!CONT3A    TZ,T1     HEAD,X5         MP
)@@G@@  . ->XXXX CASE?  @D@@@,CONT6     TZ,T1     HEAD,X5           . ->XXXX CMQ
)@@G@@ASE?  @B@,@!          J         CONT3B            . NO@B@@@,          J MR
)@@G@@        CONT7             . NO@E@,@!          SP1       KPRINT          MS
)@@G@@  . YES, SET PRINT KEY  @F@,@!          L,T2      A1,HEAD,X5        . LOMT
)@@G@@OK FOR MATCH ON STRING 2@G@@@,          L,T2      A1,HEAD,X5        . YEMU
)@@G@@S, LOOK FOR MATCH ON STRING 2 @ @@@!          LMJ       X10,SLIDE @F@@@!MV
)@@G@@          J         MATCH             . NO MATCH, KEEP PRINTING   @F@@@!MW
)@@G@@          SZ        HEAD,X5           . MATCH FOUND, CLEAR ENTRY  @ @@@!MX
)@@G@@          J         MATCH     @E@,@!CONT3B    L,T1      A1,HEAD,X5      MY
)@@G@@  . COMPARE STRING 1    @E@@@,CONT7     L,T1      A1,HEAD,X5        . COMZ
)@@G@@MPARE STRING 1    @ @@@!          LMJ       X10,SLIDE @F@@@!          J NA
)@@G@@        ELOOP4            . NO MATCH, TRY NEXT HEADING@E@@@!          TZNB
)@@G@@,T2     HEAD,X5           . MATCH, XX-> CASE?   @B@,@!          J       NC
)@@G@@  CONT3C            . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT8             . NOND
)@@G@@@F@@@!          SP1       PRINTALL          . YES, SET PRINT ALL KEY    NE
)@@G@@@D@@@!          SZ        HEAD,X5           . CLEAR ENTRY   @ @@@!      NF
)@@G@@    J         MATCH     @G@,@!CONT3C    SP1       KPRINT            . XXNG
)@@G@@X->YYY CASE, SET PRINT KEY    @F@,@!          SZ,T1     HEAD,X5         NH
)@@G@@  . CLEAR STRING 1 PORTION    @H@@@,CONT8     SZ,T1     HEAD,X5         NI
)@@G@@  . XXX->YYY CASE, CLEAR STRING 1 PORTION @ @@@!          J         MATCNJ
)@@G@@H     @F@@@!ELOOP4    TLEM      X5,NHEAD          . ANY INPUT HEADINGS LNK
)@@G@@EFT?  @E@@@!          J         LOOP4             . YES, TRY NEXT ONE   NL
)@@G@@@F@@@!          TNZ       ROPT              . IF 'R' OPTION, KEEP GOING NM
)@@G@@@G@@@!          TZ        KHEAD             . WERE ANY HEADINGS ENCOUNTENN
)@@G@@RED?  @F@@@!          J         LOOP3             . NO MORE HEADS, NO MANO
)@@G@@TCH   @F@@@!          J         END               . NO, NOTHING MORE TO NP
)@@G@@DO    @F@@@!MATCH     SP1       KPRINT            . MATCH FOUND, SET PRINQ
)@@G@@NT KEY@E@@@!          TZ        BATCH             . IF RUN IS BATCH,    NR
)@@G@@@G@,@!          J         CONT4             .   PRINT HEADING BEING PROCNS
)@@G@@ESSED @G@@@,          J         CONT9             .   PRINT HEADING BEINNT
)@@G@@G PROCESSED @F@@@!          LXI       X1,A0             . MOVE HEADING TNU
)@@G@@O MESSAGE   @A@@@!          L         X2,(13,MESS3)   @ @@@!          L,NV
)@@G@@S2      A0,HEAD,X5@ @@@!          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @ @@@!          A,NW
)@@G@@U       A0,13     @A@@@!          S,H1      A0,COMPKT+1     @F@@@!      NX
)@@G@@    COM$P     COMPKT            . SEND MESSAGE TO CONSOLE   @^@,@!CONT4 NY
)@@G@@    TNZ       ROPT@H@,@!          SZ        HEAD,X5           . CLEAR INNZ
)@@G@@PUT HEAD IF NOT 'R' OPTION    @F@,@!CONT5     LXI       A0,NWDS         OA
)@@G@@  . SUBMIT PRINT CONTROL IMAGE@F@@@,CONT9     LXI       A0,NWDS         OB
)@@G@@  . SUBMIT PRINT CONTROL IMAGE@ @@@!          LXM,U     A0,IMAGE  @ @@@!OC
)@@G@@          EX        EPRTCN,X3 @ @@@!          J         LOOP3     @E@@@!OD
)@@G@@DATA      TNZ       KPRINT            . IS PRINT KEY SET?   @C@@@!      OE
)@@G@@    J         LOOP3             . NO, SKIP@D@@@!          L,T2      A0,COF
)@@G@@ONTROL        . LINE SPACING  @^@@@!          LSSL      A0,6@D@@@!      OG
)@@G@@    A,S2      A0,CONTROL        . WORD COUNT    @ @@@!          LSSL    OH
)@@G@@  A0,18     @E@@@!          LXM,U     A0,IMAGE          . DATA IMAGE LOCOI
)@@G@@ATION @D@@@!          L,S6      X3,CONTROL        . CODE TYPE     @E@@@!OJ
)@@G@@          EX        EPRINT,X3         . PRINT DATA IMAGE    @ @@@!      OK
)@@G@@    J         LOOP3     @E@@@!END       PRTCN$    NOHEAD,1          . TUOL
)@@G@@RN OFF HEADING    @E@@@!          PRINT$    MESS1,NMESS1,-1   . PRINT ENOM
)@@G@@D MESSAGE   @E@@@!          LMJ       X11,POSTPR$       . CLOSE INPUT FION
)@@G@@LE    @#@@@!          ERR$    @G@@@!          L         X5,(1,0)        OO
)@@G@@  . CHECK IF ANY LEFT OVER HEADINGS @ @@@!          L,U       X1,HDBUFF OP
)@@G@@@ @@@!          L,U       X2,PRINT  @ @@@!          SZ        KHEAD     OQ
)@@G@@@ @@@!          SZ        BASCII    @ @@@!LOOP5     TNZ       HEAD,X5   OR
)@@G@@@ @@@!          J         ELOOP5    @F@@@!          TZ        KHEAD     OS
)@@G@@        . IS THIS FIRST HEADING?    @B@,@!          J         CONT6     OT
)@@G@@        . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT10            . NO@E@@@!      OU
)@@G@@    PRINT$    MESS2,NMESS2,2    . 'HEADINGS NOT FOUND'@D@@@!          PROV
)@@G@@INT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   @G@,@!CONT6     TNZ,T1    HEADOW
)@@G@@,X5           . IS HEADING OF FORM: ->XXXX ?    @G@@@,CONT10    TNZ,T1  OX
)@@G@@  HEAD,X5           . IS HEADING OF FORM: ->XXXX ?    @C@,@!          J OY
)@@G@@        CONT7             . YES     @C@@@,          J         CONT11    OZ
)@@G@@        . YES     @F@@@!          LXI,S1    X1,HEAD,X5        . NO, GET PA
)@@G@@STARTING CHAR #   @D@@@!          L,S2      A0,HEAD,X5        . GET # OFPB
)@@G@@ CHARS@ @@@!          TZ,T2     HEAD,X5   @G@@@!          A,S4      A0,HPC
)@@G@@EAD,X5        . ADD # OF CHARS IN 2ND STRING    @G@@@!          TZ,S4   PD
)@@G@@  HEAD,X5           . IS HEADING A SINGULAR STRING?   @F@@@!          A,PE
)@@G@@U       A0,2              . NO, ADD 2 CHARS FOR '->'  @ @,@!          J PF
)@@G@@        CONT8     @ @@@,          J         CONT12    @E@,@!CONT7     LXPG
)@@G@@I,S3    X1,HEAD,X5        . GET STARTING CHAR # @E@@@,CONT11    LXI,S3  PH
)@@G@@  X1,HEAD,X5        . GET STARTING CHAR # @D@@@!          AN        X1,(PI
)@@G@@2,0)          . BACKUP TO '->'@D@@@!          L,S4      A0,HEAD,X5      PJ
)@@G@@  . GET # OF CHARS@D@@@!          A,U       A0,2              . ADD 2 FOPK
)@@G@@R '->'@G@,@!CONT8     LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE STRING TO PRINTPL
)@@G@@ BUFFER     @G@@@,CONT12    LMJ       X11,BMOVE         . MOVE STRING TOPM
)@@G@@ PRINT BUFFER     @G@@@!          S,H1      A0,PSYMB+4        . STORE # PN
)@@G@@OF CHAR IN SYMB$ PKT    @ @@@!          L,U       A0,PSYMB  @D@@@!      PO
)@@G@@    ER        SYMB$             . PRINT HEADING @C@@@!          SP1     PP
)@@G@@  KHEAD             . SET KEY @ @@@!ELOOP5    TLEM      X5,NHEAD  @ @@@!PQ
)@@G@@          J         LOOP5     @C@@@!          EXIT$                     PR
)@@G@@  . EXIT    @A@\@!ERR1      PRINT$    MESS4,NMESS4    @#@\@!          EXPS
)@@G@@IT$   @D@@@!ERR2      TE,U      A5,1              . WAS EOF READ? @E@@@!PT
)@@G@@          J         ERR2A             . NO, OTHER I/O ERROR @F@@@!      PU
)@@G@@    TZ        SWAP              . WAS TAPE JUST SWAPPED?    @D@@@!      PV
)@@G@@    ERR$                        . YES, ERROR    @E@@@!          IOW$    PW
)@@G@@  IOPKT             . READ NEXT RECORD    @ @@@!          L,S1      A0,IPX
)@@G@@MAGE  @G@@@!          TE,U      A0,054            . IS IT AN END-OF-REELPY
)@@G@@ RECORD?    @C@@@!          J         END               . NO, STOP@F@@@!PZ
)@@G@@          TSWAP$    IOPKT             . YES, SWAP TO NEXT REEL    @D@@@!QA
)@@G@@          S         A0,SWAP           . SET SWAP KEY  @E@@@!          PRQB
)@@G@@INT$    MESS6,NMESS6,2    . 'TAPE SWAPPED .....'@E@@@!          J       QC
)@@G@@  INIT              . RE-INITIALIZE SIR$  @A@@@!ERR2A     PRINT$    MESSQD
)@@G@@5,NMESS5    @#@@@!          EXIT$   @H@@@!. ****************************QE
)@@G@@**********************************************  @H@@@!. ******* SLIDE HEQF
)@@G@@ADING PAST PRINT CONTROL IMAGE SUBROUTINE          *******  @H@@@!. ****QG
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  QH
)@@G@@@H@@@!. ******* INPUT A1= 0,0,SC,NC                                     QI
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. *******                                             QJ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@!. ****************************************QK
)@@G@@**********************************  @E@@@!SLIDE     DSL       A1,6      QL
)@@G@@        . ISOLATE # OF CHARS  @ @@@!          SSL       A2,30     @E@@@!QM
)@@G@@          LXI,S1    X2,A1             . GET STARTING CHAR # @G@@@!      QN
)@@G@@    L         A1,NCHAR          . # OF CHARS IN PRINT CONTROL     @G@@@!QO
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,FINDFIELD     . SLIDE HEADING PAST PRINT CONTROLQP
)@@G@@@C@@@!          J         0,X10             . NO FIND @D@@@!          J QQ

)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ******** THIS PDP ELEMENT CONTAINS USEFUL PROCS NOT DEFINED BY TXQ
)@@G@@HE *******  @H@@@Q. ******** EXEC 8.  THESE PROCS ARE MADE AVAILABLE TO XR
)@@G@@THE USER BY    *******  @H@@@Q. ******** INVOKING THE PROC 'LIPROCS'.  IXS
)@@G@@F THIS ELEMENT HAS NOT BEEN*******  @H@@@Q. ******** INCORPORATED INTO TXT
)@@G@@HE OPERATING SYSTEM, IT FIRST MUST BE  *******  @H@@@Q. ******** PDP'ED XU
)@@G@@INTO THE FILE FROM WHICH THE CALLING PROGRAM IS    *******  @H@@@Q. ****XV
)@@G@@**** BEING ASSEMBLED.                                          *******  XW
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********                                                        XX
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ****************************************************XY
)@@G@@**********************  @D@@@QLIPROC$*  $PROC     0                 . MAXZ
)@@G@@STER PROC   @D@@@QLIPROCS*  $NAME                       . ALTERNATE NAMEYA
)@@G@@@H@T@Q          AXR$                        . STANDARD ASSEMBLER REGISTEYB
)@@G@@R NAMES     @H@@@T          $INCLUDE  'MAXR$/'          . STANDARD ASSEMYC
)@@G@@BLER REGISTER NAMES     @H@@@Q. ****************************************YD
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@Q. ******** CHECK XQT OPTION $PYE
)@@G@@ROC- ISOLATES BIT CORR. TO INPUT LETTER*******  @H@@@Q. ********        YF
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@Q. ****YG
)@@G@@**** E.G.  TOPT 'U'    = AND A0,(000000000040)                 *******  YH
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********       TOPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000000000040)              YI
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ********       AOPT 'U'    = AND A0,(000000000040)  YJ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ********       AOPT A2,'U' = AND A2,(000YK
)@@G@@000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       SOPT 'U'    =YL
)@@G@@ TOP A0,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********       SYM
)@@G@@OPT A2,'U' = TOP A2,(000000000040)                 *******  @H@@@Q. ****YN
)@@G@@****       GOPT 'U'    = ER OPT$                               *******  YO
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********                     AND A0,(000000000040)              YP
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ****************************************************YQ
)@@G@@**********************  @#@@@QP         $PROC   @^@@@QTOPT**    $NAME   YR
)@@G@@  0   @^@@@QAOPT**    $NAME     0   @^@@@QGOPT**    $NAME     1   @^@@@QYS
)@@G@@SOPT**    $NAME     2   @A@@@Q          $DO P(0,0)=1 , ER OPT$    @F@@@QYT
)@@G@@          $DO (P(0,0)<2)**(P(1)=1) , AND A0,(1*/('Z'-P(1,1)))     @F@@@QYU
)@@G@@          $DO (P(0,0)=0)**(P(1)>1) , AND P(1,1),(1*/('Z'-P(1,2))) @F@@@QYV
)@@G@@          $DO (P(0,0)=2)**(P(1)=1) , TOP A0,(1*/('Z'-P(1,1)))     @F@@@QYW
)@@G@@          $DO (P(0,0)=2)**(P(1)>1) , TOP P(1,1),(1*/('Z'-P(1,2))) @#@@@QYX
)@@G@@          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. **********************************YY
)@@G@@****************************************  @H@@@Q. ******** FORTRAN CALL YZ
)@@G@@$PROC                                        *******  @H@@@Q. ********  ZA
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@QZB
)@@G@@. ******** CALL SUBR A,B,C,D  = LMJ X11,SUBR                         ***ZC
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********                      + A                         ZD
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ********                      + B             ZE
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. ********                      + C ZF
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ********              ZG
)@@G@@        + D                                  *******  @H@@@Q. ********  ZH
)@@G@@                    + 0                                  *******  @H@@@QZI
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************ZJ
)@@G@@****  @#@@@QCALL**    $PROC   @A@@@Q          LMJ       X11,CALL(1,1)   ZK
)@@G@@@A@@@QI         $DO CALL(2) , + CALL(2,I) @^@@@Q          +         0   ZL
)@@G@@@#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@Q. ****************************ZM
)@@G@@**********************************************  @H@@@Q. ******** INFOR TZN
)@@G@@ABLE INTERFACE PROCS - AIDS IN USING RINF$, SELT$  *******  @H@@@Q. ****ZO
)@@G@@****               AND DUSE$ SUBROUTINES                       *******  ZP
)@@G@@@H@@@Q. ********                                                        ZQ
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@Q. ******** R$INF - CALLS 'RINF$' AND INVOKES 'ELT$'   ZR
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$ELT - CALLS 'SELT$' WITH PARAZS
)@@G@@METER #                    *******  @H@@@Q. ******** D$USE - CALLS 'DUSEZT
)@@G@@$' WITH FILE$NAME(MAY BE R.J.)         *******  @H@@@Q. ****************ZU
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@QP     ZV
)@@G@@    $PROC     1    . A PARAMETER SPECIFIES # OF XQT PARAMETERS EXPECTED,ZW
)@@G@@@D@@@QR$INF**   $NAME          .      OTHERWISE 3 ASSUMED   @F@@@Q      ZX
)@@G@@    $LEVEL    0,1,0             . MAKE ELT$ LABELS GLOBAL   @E@@@Q      ZY
)@@G@@    ELT$                        . INVOKE 'ELT$' PROC  @F@@@Q          $LZZ
)@@G@@EVEL    0,0,0             . RETURN TO NORMAL LEVELING @B@@@QNN        $EAA
)@@G@@QU      28*(3*(P=1)+P(1,1))   @A@@@Q          L         A0,(NN,INF)     AB
)@@G@@@ @@@Q          LMJ       X11,RINF$ @^@@@Q          J         ERR @^@@@QAC
)@@G@@          J         CONT@^@@@QINF       RES       NN  @ @@@QERR       ERAD
)@@G@@        PRINT$    @ @@@Q          ER        EXIT$     @]@@@QCONT      . AE
)@@G@@@#@@@Q          $END    @^@@@QP         $PROC     1   @#@@@QS$ELT**   $NAF
)@@G@@AME   @A@@@Q          $DO P(1)>0 , L,U A0,P(1,1)@^@@@Q          LMJ X11,AG
)@@G@@SELT$ @#@@@Q          $END    @^@@@QP         $PROC     1   @#@@@QD$USE*AH
)@@G@@*   $NAME   @C@@@Q          $DO P(1)>0 , DL A0,($CFS(P(1,1)DL))   @ @@@QAI
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,DUSE$ @#@@@Q          $END    @[@@@Q.     @H@@@QAJ
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************AK
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ******** SOURCE OUTPUT PROCS - AIDS IN USING SSOR, SOR, ANAL
)@@G@@D ESOR   *******  @H@@@Q. ********                       SUBROUTINES    AM
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@Q. ********                          AN
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@Q. ******** S$SOR - SETS AO
)@@G@@UP 'PARTBL', ASSIGNS FILE AND CALLS 'SSOR'   *******  @H@@@Q. ********  AP
)@@G@@       P(1,1) =   FILE $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)                *******  @H@@@QAQ
)@@G@@. ********         P(1,2) = ELEMENT $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)               ***AR
)@@G@@****  @H@@@Q. ********         P(1,3) = VERSION $NAME(MAY BE R.J.)      AS
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@Q. ********         P(0,1) = 1, IF NOT FIRST TIMEAT

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF**[@@@@CTS@[=@ @@@@      SUBROUTINE SORTRF(RT,EP)*[@@@@CTS@[,YL
)@@G@@@^@@@@      PARAMETER LEN=5000*[@@@@CTS@[8@ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER (YM
)@@G@@A-Z)  *[@@@@CTS@]]@A@@@@      FD(I,K)=FLD(IABS(6*I-6),6,K)  *[@@@@CTS@]GYN
)@@G@@@^@@@@      H1(I)=FLD(0,18,I) *[@@@@CTS@]Q@E@@@@      COMMON A(LEN,8),NDYO
)@@G@@X(LEN),WORK(LEN),BUF(22),B(6),IC,IW *[@@@@CTS@])@B@@@@      IF (RT.GT.LEYP
)@@G@@N.OR.EP.GT.LEN) GO TO 55*[@@@@CTS@]%@B@@@@      IF (RT.EQ.0.OR.EP.EQ.0) YQ
)@@G@@GO TO 55    *[@@@@CTS@]4@C@@@@      CALL BUF2(4,0,0,0)   @ START INPUT OYR
)@@G@@N 2   *[@@@@CTS@]"@#@@@@      DO 10 I=1,RT*[@@@@CTS@#C@B@@@@   10 CALL BYS
)@@G@@UF2(5,A(I,1),6,LEN)  @ INPUT  *[@@@@CTS@#M@B@@@@C     CALL NTRAN(2,22,10YT
)@@G@@)   @ REWIND 2    *[@@@@CTS@#W@ @@@@      CALL REWN (2) @ REWIND 2*[@@@@YU
)@@G@@CTS@#&@C@@@@      CALL BUF2(1,0,0,0)    @ START OUTPUT ON 2 *[@@@@CTS@#0YV
)@@G@@@#@@@@      NDX(1)=1    *[@@@@CTS@#'@D@@@@      IF (RT.GT.1) CALL SORTX(YW
)@@G@@-RT,NDX,WORK,A(1,5))    *[@@@@CTS@^^@#@@@@      DO 15 I=1,RT*[@@@@CTS@^IYX
)@@G@@@#@@@@      N=NDX(I)    *[@@@@CTS@^S@D@@@@   15 CALL BUF2(2,A(N,1),6,LENYY
)@@G@@)  @ WRITE EXT. REF'S   *[@@@@CTS@^+@B@@@@      CALL BUF2(3,0,0,0)   @ SYZ
)@@G@@TOP OUTPUT  *[@@@@CTS@^?@B@@@@C     CALL NTRAN(2,22,10)     @ REWIND 2  ZA
)@@G@@*[@@@@CTS@^6@ @@@@      CALL REWN (2) @ REWIND 2*[@@@@CTS@ @@B@@@@      ZB
)@@G@@CALL BUF3(4,0,0,0)   @ START INPUT  *[@@@@CTS@ E@C@@@@      CALL BUF2(4,ZC
)@@G@@0,0,0)    @ START INPUT ON 2  *[@@@@CTS@ O@#@@@@      DO 20 I=1,EP*[@@@@ZD
)@@G@@CTS@ Y@B@@@@   20 CALL BUF3(5,A(I,1),8,LEN)   @ INPUT *[@@@@CTS@ *@#@@@@ZE
)@@G@@      NDX(1)=1    *[@@@@CTS@ 2@D@@@@      IF (EP.GT.1) CALL SORTX(-EP,NDZF
)@@G@@X,WORK,A(1,5))    *[@@@@CTS@ /@#@@@@      CALL START  *[@@@@CTS@AA@]@@@@ZG
)@@G@@      KGO=1 *[@@@@CTS@AK@]@@@@      IRT=0 *[@@@@CTS@AU@#@@@@      DO 50 ZH
)@@G@@I=1,EP*[@@@@CTS@A=@#@@@@      J=NDX(I)    *[@@@@CTS@A,@^@@@@      LC=H1(ZI
)@@G@@A(J,7))     *[@@@@CTS@A8@C@@@@      ENCODE (25,BUF)A(J,5),A(J,6),LC,A(J,ZJ
)@@G@@8)    *[@@@@CTS@B]@B@@@@   25 FORMAT(1X,2A6,2X,O2,' (',O6,') (')  *[@@@@ZK
)@@G@@CTS@BG@#@@@@      CALL EPNAME *[@@@@CTS@BQ@^@@@@      GO TO (30,46),KGO ZL
)@@G@@*[@@@@CTS@B)@#@@@@   30 IRT=IRT+1   *[@@@@CTS@B%@ @@@@      IF (IRT.GT.RZM
)@@G@@T) GO TO 50 *[@@@@CTS@B4@A@@@@      CALL BUF2(5,B,6,1)    @ INPUT *[@@@@ZN
